# Terraform Module Standards

## Objective
Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Recommendations

  type        = string

  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}

Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl
variable "bucket_name" {
  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```

# Terraform Module Standards

## Objective
Maintain consistency and reusability through well-defined modules.

## Recommendations
- Use `variables.tf`, `outputs.tf`, and `README.md` in all modules.
- Version modules using tags.
- Validate modules with `terraform validate`.

## Example
```hcl

  description = "Name of the S3 bucket"
  type        = string
}

output "bucket_name" {
  value = aws_s3_bucket.main.bucket
}
```
